CODE RED TR COMMAND / RULE INDEX
Clean content + zombie + tune TR reference
================================================================================

Purpose
-------
One-file reference of clean .tr behavior vocabulary for Code RED AI work. This is an index, not a patch. It catalogs programs, rules, debuggroups, includes, unique predicates/actions, and high-value rule patterns so we can reuse existing behavior without guessing.

Source policy
-------------
- Used clean extracted content AI from logs.zip.
- Used clean ZombiePack TR from logs.zip.
- Used tune AI TR from tools.zip replacement set.
- Ignored our experimental TR command passes so this stays clean.
- This file contains summaries/index lines only; keep raw game files private.

Current understanding notes
---------------------------
[TR syntax]
- The actor running the brain is implicit: read bare predicates/actions as applying to “me / this AI actor”.
- x, y, z are variables bound by the predicates in that rule. Player(x) means x is the player; Enemy(x) means x is some actor I classify as enemy.
- Left of -> is condition/precondition. Right of -> is a derived fact, behavior program, or action request. Do not assume every RHS predicate safely sets engine state.
- Lines such as InSquad -> SquadMain check that the actor is already in squad state. They do not recruit the actor.
- Debuggroup/filter/predicate/label blocks appear diagnostic. Preserve them when editing, but do not treat them as behavior activators unless later proven.
- Programs and rules are evaluated by an action arbitration system. Broad edits in Main/Unalerted can freeze actors or make them run around, as our earlier tests proved.

[Safe reuse rules]
- Reuse existing programs/actions by causing the correct objective/task/squad state, instead of forcing behavior globally from Main.
- Prefer WSC/native task assignment for follow/guard/mount, then let tasks.tr/game_main.tr execute it.
- Avoid global removal of HotspotSeekToFulfillMotives; it is ambient town behavior and can break daily life AI.
- Avoid deriving InSquad, SquadLeader, HasTask, HasMoveObjective, ObjectClassObjectiveFollow blindly unless a donor mission proves it is safe.
- Patch the active override layer. The tune/ai files may override content/ai equivalents when the path/name matches.

[Companion research understanding]
- 638 ACTOR_misc_son is team-safe in testing, so faction is mostly solved for that actor.
- If a team-safe actor walks to hotspots, that likely means no active follow/squad/task objective is present, not that faction is wrong.
- The squad rules already contain defend-leader and follow-leader logic, but require real InSquad/SquadLeader/SquadAllowAttack state.
- The practical target is to find mission WSC/native calls that assign squad/follow objectives, then reuse them for cheat-spawned companions.
